infrastructure in Grafana spans multiple layers of integration across GitHub, Go backend, Kubernetes-style APIs, and JavaScript tooling. At the core is .github/CODEOWNERS, the GitHub ownership definition file. This is validated in CI by the codeowners-validator workflow (.github/workflows/codeowners-validator.yml), which runs checks for proper syntax, duplicate patterns, and unowned files. The feature management system (pkg/services/featuremgmt/) integrates CODEOWNERS with feature flags through three key components: codeowners.go defines the codeowner type and constants for all GitHub teams and users (e.g., @grafana/dashboards-squad), registry.go is where feature toggles are registered with their respective codeowner assignments, and models.go contains the FeatureFlag structure with an Owner field of type codeowner. The toggles_gen_test.go file orchestrates code generation that creates toggles_gen.go (Go constants), toggles_gen.json (JSON manifest for API servers), toggles_gen.csv (CSV export), and toggles-gitlog.csv (historical tracking). The Kubernetes-style API layer (pkg/apis/featuretoggle/v0alpha1/) exposes feature ownership through types.go (which defines the FeatureSpec.Owner field as 'codeowner'), register.go, and generated files (zz_generated.*). The registry APIs layer (pkg/registry/apis/featuretoggle/features.go) integrates the embedded feature list into the API server. On the JavaScript side, generateBettererIssues.ts uses the npm codeowners package (declared in package.json with yarn.lock versioning) to parse the CODEOWNERS file and assign code quality issues to responsible teams. The build orchestration happens through the Makefile's gen-feature-toggles target, which runs Go tests to regenerate manifests, and npm scripts like betterer:issues that leverage the codeowners library. Documentation in contribute/feature-toggles.md guides developers on defining features with proper codeowner assignments. Together, these files form a complete infrastructure for code ownership that spans from GitHub's CODEOWNERS format through feature flag management, API schemas, and issue routing.\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":12,"cache_creation_input_tokens":3340,"cache_read_input_tokens":65452,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":3340},"output_tokens":4,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"cccfcd90-e2e8-4a43-94c5-e9d7c72f2faf","uuid":"a34e23af-311a-421c-89e5-4adc7f657d75"}
